[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[39mat [0m[1;35morg.apache.poi.POIXSSFFuzzer.fuzzerTestOneInput[0m[1;39m([0m[39mPOIXSSFFuzzer.jav[0m[1;92ma:50[0m[1;39m)[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mDEDUP_TOKEN: d9d032fd1efaa9d3[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m== libFuzzer crashing input ==[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m===Evaluation [0m[33mReport[0m[39m===[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m# Evaluation Report[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Summary[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mA Server Side Request Forgery [0m[1;39m([0m[39mSSRF[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m vulnerability has been detected in Apache [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mPOI's XSSFEventBasedExcelExtractor during XML parsing operations. The fuzzer [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39midentified an attempted connection to [0m[32m"jazze.com:80"[0m[39m while processing XSSF [0m[1;39m([0m[39mExcel[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfiles, indicating that untrusted data from the input file is being used to initiate[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnetwork connections without proper validation. This vulnerability is classified as [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39ma medium-severity security issue that could lead to exfiltration of sensitive data [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mor exposure of internal services.[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe issue manifests as a Server Side Request Forgery [0m[1;39m([0m[39mSSRF[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m vulnerability during [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe processing of XSSF Excel files. The security issue was detected by the Jazzer [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfuzzer's SSRF sanitizer at `[0m[1;35mServerSideRequestForgery.checkSsrf[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`, which monitors [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mand flags potentially dangerous network connections initiated from untrusted [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msources.[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Vulnerability Type[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis is a Server Side Request Forgery [0m[1;39m([0m[39mSSRF[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m vulnerability, where an application [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmakes requests to external or internal resources based on user-controlled data [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwithout proper validation. SSRF vulnerabilities can be exploited to:[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Access internal services that should not be publicly accessible[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Exfiltrate sensitive data from internal networks[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Perform port scanning of internal infrastructure[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Bypass firewall restrictions[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Access cloud metadata services in cloud environments[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Key Observations[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Attack Vector**: The vulnerability is triggered through XML entity processing [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mduring XSSF file parsing. The stack trace shows the connection attempt originates [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfrom XML entity resolution in the Xerces XML parser [0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m`[0m[1;35mXMLEntityManager.setupCurrentEntity[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Execution Flow**: The vulnerable path follows this sequence:[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `[0m[1;35mPOIXSSFFuzzer.fuzzerTestOneInput[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` → Entry point for fuzzing[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `[0m[1;35mPOIFuzzer.checkExtractor[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` → Extraction logic[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `[0m[1;35mXSSFEventBasedExcelExtractor.getText[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` → Main text extraction[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `[0m[1;35mXSSFEventBasedExcelExtractor.getExtendedProps[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` → Extended properties [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mretrieval[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `[0m[1;35mSAXParser.parse[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` → XML parsing[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `XMLEntityManager` → Entity resolution leading to network connection[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Network Connection Details**: The attempted connection to [0m[32m"jazze.com:80"[0m[39m was [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mintercepted at the socket level [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`[0m[1;35mjava.net.Socket.connect[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, indicating that the [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mXML parser is attempting to resolve and fetch external entities defined in the XSSF[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfile.[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Root Cause Location**: The issue originates in the XML parsing layer, [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mspecifically during entity resolution in [0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mXSSFEventBasedExcelExtractor.getExtendedProps[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` at line [0m[1;36m316[0m[39m, where a SAXParser is[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mused without secure configuration to prevent external entity resolution.[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Areas Requiring Investigation[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mTo gain a comprehensive understanding of this vulnerability, the following [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcomponents should be investigated:[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **XSSFEventBasedExcelExtractor Class**:[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The `[0m[1;35mgetExtendedProps[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` method [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m316[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m where XML parsing occurs[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The `[0m[1;35mgetText[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` method [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m299[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m which calls `[0m[1;35mgetExtendedProps[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - How SAXParser instances are configured and whether XXE [0m[1;39m([0m[39mXML External Entity[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprotections are enabled[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - All locations where XML parsing occurs within this class[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **XML Parser Configuration**:[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Review how SAXParser and other XML parsers are instantiated throughout Apache [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mPOI[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Check for the presence [0m[1;39m([0m[39mor absence[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m of security features such as:[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     - `FEATURE_SECURE_PROCESSING`[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     - Disabling DOCTYPE declarations[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     - Disabling external general entities[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     - Disabling external parameter entities[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     - Disabling external DTDs[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Other XSSF Components**:[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Similar XML parsing operations in related XSSF classes[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Any other extractors or processors that handle XSSF files[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Document property readers and metadata extractors[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Input Handling**:[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - How XSSF files are validated before processing[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Whether there are existing input sanitization mechanisms[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The structure of XSSF files that could contain malicious entity declarations[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **POI Package-Wide Review**:[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Survey all XML parsing operations across the Apache POI codebase[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Identify other file format handlers [0m[1;39m([0m[39mHSSF, SXSSF, etc.[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m that may have similar [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvulnerabilities[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Review centralized XML parser factory methods or utilities[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis vulnerability represents a classic XXE [0m[1;39m([0m[39mXML External Entity[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m attack vector [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthat manifests as SSRF, where maliciously crafted XSSF files containing external [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mentity references can cause the application to make arbitrary network requests to [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mattacker-controlled or internal destinations.[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. Core Analysis[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m#### Root Cause[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe vulnerability exists in `[0m[1;35mXSSFEventBasedExcelExtractor.getExtendedProps[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` at [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mline [0m[1;36m315[0m[39m, where a SAXParser is created using:[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```java[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mSAXParser parser = [0m[1;35mSAXParserFactory.newInstance[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.newSAXParser[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis creates an unsecured SAXParser without any XXE/SSRF protections, allowing [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexternal entity resolution that leads to Server Side Request Forgery attacks.[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m#### Evidence from Code Analysis[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Secure Pattern Already Used**: The same class uses `[0m[1;35mXMLHelper.newXMLReader[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mat line [0m[1;36m251[0m[39m in the `[0m[1;35mprocessSheet[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` method, demonstrating that developers were [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39maware of secure parsing practices but missed applying them to `[0m[1;35mgetExtendedProps[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`.[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **XMLHelper Infrastructure Available**: The class already imports `XMLHelper` at [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mline [0m[1;36m48[0m[39m but doesn't use it for extended properties parsing.[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Comprehensive Security Features**: XMLHelper provides complete XXE/SSRF [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprotection through:[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  - FEATURE_SECURE_PROCESSING enabled[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  - FEATURE_EXTERNAL_ENTITIES disabled[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  - FEATURE_DISALLOW_DOCTYPE_DECL enabled[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  - Entity resolver that ignores external entities[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  - Xerces security manager with entity expansion limit of [0m[1;36m1[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. Fix Implementation Strategy[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m#### Option [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m: Use [0m[1;35mXMLHelper.newXMLReader[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mRECOMMENDED[0m[1;39m)[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mReplace lines [0m[1;36m314[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m316[0m[39m in `[0m[1;35mXSSFEventBasedExcelExtractor.getExtendedProps[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` with:[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```java[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtry [0m[1;39m([0m[39mInputStream is = [0m[1;35mpart.getInputStream[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    XMLReader xmlReader = [0m[1;35mXMLHelper.newXMLReader[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;35mxmlReader.setContentHandler[0m[1;39m([0m[39mnew [0m[1;35mExtendedPropertiesHandler[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtext[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;35mxmlReader.parse[0m[1;39m([0m[39mnew [0m[1;35mInputSource[0m[1;39m([0m[39mis[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m}[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Rationale**: This is the most secure approach as it provides:[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- All security features from the secure SAXParserFactory[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Additional entity resolver that returns empty InputSource for external entities[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Custom error handler for better error reporting[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Direct FEATURE_SECURE_PROCESSING and FEATURE_EXTERNAL_ENTITIES configuration on [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe XMLReader[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Xerces security manager or entity expansion limit[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m#### Option [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m: Use [0m[1;35mXMLHelper.getSaxParserFactory[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mALTERNATIVE[0m[1;39m)[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mReplace line [0m[1;36m315[0m[39m with:[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```java[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mSAXParser parser = [0m[1;35mXMLHelper.getSaxParserFactory[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.newSAXParser[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Rationale**: This provides all security features from the factory configuration [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwhile maintaining the existing code structure with minimal changes.[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. Recommended Approach[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Use Option [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mXMLHelper.newXMLReader[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m** for the following reasons:[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Consistency with Existing Code**: The `[0m[1;35mprocessSheet[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` method at line [0m[1;36m251[0m[39m [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39malready uses `[0m[1;35mXMLHelper.newXMLReader[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`, so using the same pattern in [0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mgetExtendedProps[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` maintains consistency.[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Defense in Depth**: [0m[1;35mXMLHelper.newXMLReader[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m provides multiple layers of [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprotection:[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Secure SAXParserFactory configuration[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Entity resolver [0m[1;39m([0m[39mXMLHelper::ignoreEntity[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m that prevents entity resolution even[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mif features fail[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Additional security features set directly on XMLReader[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Xerces security manager for entity expansion limits[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Best Practice**: The codebase tests [0m[1;39m([0m[39mTestXMLHelper[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m validate that [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mnewXMLReader[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m provides complete security configuration, making it the established [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbest practice.[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Minimal Code Changes**: Only requires modifying the try block content [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m314[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m316[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, with no changes to imports, exception handling, or the [0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mExtendedPropertiesHandler class.[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m. Implementation Steps[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Step [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m**: Modify the `[0m[1;35mgetExtendedProps[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` method in [0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`poi-ooxml/src/main/java/org/apache/poi/xssf/extractor/XSSFEventBasedExcelExtractor[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m.java`:[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Locate lines [0m[1;36m314[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m316[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Replace the vulnerable SAXParser creation with [0m[1;35mXMLHelper.newXMLReader[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Convert the DefaultHandler usage to ContentHandler pattern with InputSource[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Ensure the ExtendedPropertiesHandler extends DefaultHandler [0m[1;39m([0m[39mwhich implements [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mContentHandler[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, so no changes needed to the handler class[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Step [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m**: Verify imports are correct:[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- `XMLHelper` is already imported at line [0m[1;36m48[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- `InputSource` is already imported at line [0m[1;36m63[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- `XMLReader` is already imported at line [0m[1;36m65[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- No new imports needed[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Step [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m**: Maintain exception handling:[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Keep the existing try-catch block structure[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The ParserConfigurationException should remain in the catch clause as [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mXMLHelper.newXMLReader[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m can throw it[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- All existing exception handling remains unchanged[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m5[0m[39m. Justification[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m#### Why This Is Optimal[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Fixes the Root Cause**: Replaces insecure XML parsing with secure parsing that[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprevents XXE/SSRF attacks.[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Maintains Existing Functionality**: The ExtendedPropertiesHandler works [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39midentically whether used with [0m[1;35mSAXParser.parse[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m or [0m[1;35mXMLReader.parse[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, since [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mDefaultHandler implements ContentHandler.[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **No Breaking Changes**: [0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Same text extraction behavior[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Same exception handling[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Same API surface[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - ExtendedPropertiesHandler requires no modifications[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Follows Established Patterns**: Aligns with the secure pattern already used in[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mprocessSheet[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m method in the same class.[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **Comprehensive Protection**: Provides multiple layers of defense against [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mXXE/SSRF attacks through XMLHelper's carefully configured security features.[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m#### How It Preserves Existing Logic[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Text Extraction**: The ExtendedPropertiesHandler continues to extract text [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfrom extended properties XML elements in exactly the same way.[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Error Handling**: The try-catch block continues to catch and swallow [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mParserConfigurationException, SAXException, and IOException as before.[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **API Compatibility**: The [0m[1;35mgetText[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m method that calls [0m[1;35mgetExtendedProps[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m at [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mline [0m[1;36m299[0m[39m remains unchanged, and all callers continue to work identically.[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **No Behavioral Changes**: The only change is in how the XML parser is [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mconfigured for security; the parsing behavior and output remain identical for [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlegitimate files.[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m#### How It Addresses the Issue[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Prevents External Entity Resolution**: The secure configuration disables [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexternal entities, preventing the parser from making network connections to [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mattacker-controlled URLs [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlike [0m[32m"jazze.com:80"[0m[39m in the fuzzer report[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Blocks DOCTYPE Declarations**: FEATURE_DISALLOW_DOCTYPE_DECL prevents DOCTYPE [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdeclarations that could be used for XXE attacks.[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Limits Entity Expansion**: Entity expansion limit of [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m prevents entity [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexpansion DoS attacks.[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Defense in Depth**: The entity resolver [0m[1;39m([0m[39mignoreEntity[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m provides an additional [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlayer that returns empty InputSource for any entity resolution attempts, ensuring [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprotection even if other features fail.[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m6[0m[39m. Potential Side Effects and Mitigation[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m#### Side Effects[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Legitimate External Entities**: If any legitimate XSSF files use external [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mentities in extended properties [0m[1;39m([0m[39mhighly unlikely as this violates OOXML [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mspecification[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, they would fail to parse.[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Mitigation**: This is desired behavior from a security perspective. Extended[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mproperties should not contain external entity references.[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Performance**: The secure configuration adds minimal overhead for entity [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mresolution checks.[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Mitigation**: The overhead is negligible and acceptable for security [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbenefits.[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Parser Compatibility**: Older XML parsers might not support all security [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfeatures.[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Mitigation**: XMLHelper uses [0m[1;35mtrySet[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m methods that gracefully handle [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39munsupported features without throwing exceptions, ensuring compatibility.[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m#### Testing Considerations[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. The fix should not break existing tests, as legitimate XSSF files don't use [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexternal entities in extended properties.[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. The existing test [0m[32m"testXXEInSchema"[0m[39m demonstrates that XXE prevention is expected[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbehavior in the codebase.[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. The fuzzer that detected this issue should no longer trigger SSRF warnings after[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe fix.[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m7[0m[39m. Similar Solutions in Codebase[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe codebase already demonstrates this pattern multiple times:[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **[0m[1;35mXSSFEventBasedExcelExtractor.processSheet[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m251[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m: Uses [0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mXMLHelper.newXMLReader[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **TestXSSFSheetXMLHandler** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m45[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m81[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m: Uses [0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mXMLHelper.getSaxParserFactory[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.newSAXParser[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.getXMLReader[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **ExcelFileFormatDocFunctionExtractor** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m435[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m: Uses [0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mXMLHelper.getSaxParserFactory[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis fix applies the same established secure pattern to the overlooked [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mgetExtendedProps[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m method.[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m. Conclusion[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis fix strategy provides a minimal, focused change that:[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Addresses the SSRF vulnerability completely[0m                                       [2m                [0m
